  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6097964f-cbe2-46a5-a0f4-65bc288d045c'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<span id="freeTextContainer15764156593440810977"><b>NOTE FROM THE AUTHORS:<br/>This is the OLD version of Evenfall. An updated, heavily revised, and partially re-written edition of Evenfall can be found under <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20926065.Evenfall_Volume_1__Director_s_Cut' title='Evenfall Volume 1: Director's Cut' rel='nofollow noopener'>Evenfall Volume 1: Director's Cut</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20926136.Evenfall_Volume_2__Director_s_Cut' title='Evenfall Volume 2: Director's Cut' rel='nofollow noopener'>Evenfall Volume 2: Director's Cut</a><br/><br/>The authors strongly suggest new readers download the new edition.<br/><br/>After September 21, 2014, the old edition will no longer be available for download. :]</b></span>
  <span id="freeText15764156593440810977" style="display:none"><b>NOTE FROM THE AUTHORS:<br />This is the OLD version of Evenfall. An updated, heavily revised, and partially re-written edition of Evenfall can be found under <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20926065.Evenfall_Volume_1__Director_s_Cut" title="Evenfall Volume 1: Director's Cut" rel="nofollow noopener">Evenfall Volume 1: Director's Cut</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20926136.Evenfall_Volume_2__Director_s_Cut" title="Evenfall Volume 2: Director's Cut" rel="nofollow noopener">Evenfall Volume 2: Director's Cut</a><br /><br />The authors strongly suggest new readers download the new edition.<br /><br />After September 21, 2014, the old edition will no longer be available for download. :]</b><br />__________<br />Years after the bombs of WWIII have changed the physical and political landscape, the Agency ruthlessly works behind the scenes to take down rebel groups that threaten the current government. Their goals justify all means. Hsin Liu Vega (Sin) is their most efficient and deadly assassin ever. However, he tends to go off on unauthorized killing sprees and somehow his assigned partners all end up dead under suspicious circumstances. That is why the Agency has had him locked up in a box on the fourth floor for years. But now they think it is time to put the psychopath back in the field. With a new partner. <br /><br />Boyd's mother, a high ranking Agency official, volunteers her teenage son for the position. Boyd is not afraid of death. In fact, his life has been such an endless cycle of apathy and despair for the last few years that he'd welcome it. <br /><br />Can these two broken men form an efficient partnership? Can they learn to trust anyone, let alone each other? Sin doesn't give a fuck about the Agency, or the androgynous boy who holds the remote to the shock collar that is supposed to control him. <br /><br />On the other hand, Boyd is strangely unafraid of the man everyone calls 'monster' and Sin seems reluctant to let his keeper get himself killed on any missions. Yet.</span>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">In the comments from the authors on the site where you download these books, they state that the books have not been published. The do hope to officia<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">In the comments from the authors on the site where you download these books, they state that the books have not been published. The do hope to officially epublish them at some point and they are reworking the whole series. I'm not sure if this means they will make hard copies available though. You could always ask the authors. They are both on goodreads, and they would probably love to hear from a die hard fan.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_544171079" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/544171079" />
    <a title="Dd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9444787-dd"><img alt="Dd" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/544171079?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dd" href="/user/show/9444787-dd">Dd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9444787-dd?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer544171079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3788259286144989885"><br/><i>A book of 1427 pages!!!<br/><br/><b>Hallelujah,I finished it after hours and hours of voracious reading.</b></i><br/><br/><b>
  <u>WARNING Readers!!!</u>
</b><br/><br/><b>1)</b> In this short period of time, it changed my status from friendly and social to an anti-social biatch.It seems that two days of barely sleeping,cancelling all plans,not receiving calls,and talking in non-committable grunts can do that.<br/><br/><b>2)</b> Sin and Boyd (the main characters of this story) can try the patience of any saint,any day.<br/><br/><b>That said,together they will try the patience of God him</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3788259286144989885" style="display:none"><br /><i>A book of 1427 pages!!!<br /><br /><b>Hallelujah,I finished it after hours and hours of voracious reading.</b></i><br /><br /><b>
  <u>WARNING Readers!!!</u>
</b><br /><br /><b>1)</b> In this short period of time, it changed my status from friendly and social to an anti-social biatch.It seems that two days of barely sleeping,cancelling all plans,not receiving calls,and talking in non-committable grunts can do that.<br /><br /><b>2)</b> Sin and Boyd (the main characters of this story) can try the patience of any saint,any day.<br /><br /><b>That said,together they will try the patience of God himself!</b><br /><br /><b>3)</b> One time specifically, they gave me a major heart attack.But don't worry, other times the attacks were pretty minor ones.<br /><br /><b>4)</b> Oh,and do keep a pillow nearby to muffle your frustrated screams.It will save you from being thought of as a raving lunatic.<br /><br />Hmm...I guess that will be it,for now.<br /><br /><br /><i>Now,let me introduce you to these two irritating, gorgeous, exasperating, amazing, beautiful, lethal, stunning,....ummm,okay,I guess you got my point!!</i><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Together, Sin and Boyd are unforgettable.</i>
</b><br /><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <pre>So many and so various laws are giv’n;<br />So many laws argue so many sins.</pre>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Sins,there are so many sins of Mankind.And this book presents us with innumerable examples.<br /><br /><b>Set up in a post-war dystopian world,this book sets up a pace from the beginning which is fast,dangerous and thrilling.</b><br /><br />As I've said before,this story revolves around these two men.....<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Sin is thought of as inhuman.And Boyd is more like a robot.<br /><br />Sin has been labelled as 'Monster'.And Boyd has been labelled as 'Worthless'.<br /><br />Sin is feared by everyone,afterall he is death.Boyd does not fear death.</i>
</b><br /><br />And the relationship which grows between them,will leave you breathless.<br /><br /><br />After WWIII, several rebel groups came into play to take down the Government.So, the Agency works behind the scene to remove them.The Agency and all the agents of the Agency,stay in shadows.No one knows of their existence.<br /><br /><b>They are phantoms who get the work done and then leave the scene undetected and unnoticed.</b><br /> <br /><br />Hsin Liu Vega (Sin) is the very best they have.But,he is deemed mentally unstable.He's said to be a psychopath.He is said to go wild sometimes and kill whoever comes in contact.And all his partners end up dead,somehow.So,he is locked and caged,until need for him arises.And this time when the need arises, he is put back in the field with a new partner.<br /><br />Boyd's mother is the second in command.She nominates Boyd for the job.Boyd doesn't mind that being Sin's partner is nearly signing his own death warrant.Because he does not want to live anyway.A violent episode of his past haunts him.It had nearly killed him and took all he held dear away from him.Now, all his emotions are buried deep down.<br /><br /><br /><b>But how can these to utterly broken men,each in their own way,can ever be partners? How can they ever develop a relationship?</b><br /><br />---------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Readers,I suggest you read this book.Because it will take you through one unforgettable journey.<br /><br />Now I'm not saying that it will be a cakewalk.At times it is really annoying,at times irritating.A lot of editing could be done.Descriptions could be smaller,inner monologues could be cut down.Times when Sin and Boyd are not together could be shorter too.<br /><br />But,to be very frank,I am giving it 5 stars,because any book which can capture my attention,engross me,suck me in like this one did,deserves a 5 star rating from me.<br /><br />And lets not forget that this has 1427 pages.<b>Which means that it is nearly 5 times the length of any average book.</b><br /><br />And the fact that it did not let my attention divert even for a minute,is by itself amazing.<br /><br />Seriously,it deserves an applause.<br /><br /><br /><b>I loved this book.I wanted to start with Afterimage today,but I cannot cancel anymore classes,and I do need some sleep.Immediately.</b><br /><br />All that said....<br /><br /><i>So sleepy.</i><br /><br />....It's time for me to go.<br /><br /><br /><b>That's all for now,Readers.<br /><br />Ta-Ta!!</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3788259286144989885" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_563821866" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/563821866" />
    <a title="Julio Genao" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3977017-julio-genao"><img alt="Julio Genao" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442881106p2/3977017.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/563821866?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julio Genao" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julio Genao" href="/user/show/3977017-julio-genao">Julio Genao</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Julio by: </span>
      Taylor
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer563821866" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14677060861916073567"><i>(review of an earlier edition)</i><br/><br/><b>Why hate the sinner... when you can love the Hsin?</b><br/><br/>A month ago I read a great review of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8164593.Afterimage__In_the_Company_of_Shadows___2_' title='Afterimage (In the Company of Shadows, #2) by Santino Hassell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Afterimage</a>, <a href='http://jgenao.wordpress.com/2013/06/09/afterimage/' rel='nofollow noopener'>and blogged about it</a>, but spent most of my post whining about how much of a chickenshit motherfucker I was for not only failing to read the second volume of <i>In the Company of Shadows</i>, but not even reviewing the first one.<br/><br/>The results of the poll on that page pretty much vindicated my cowardice.<br/><br/>I read <i>Evenfall</i> not long after <i>Special Forces</i>, for one. And winter is a histo</span>
  <span id="freeText14677060861916073567" style="display:none"><i>(review of an earlier edition)</i><br /><br /><b>Why hate the sinner... when you can love the Hsin?</b><br /><br />A month ago I read a great review of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8164593.Afterimage__In_the_Company_of_Shadows___2_" title="Afterimage (In the Company of Shadows, #2) by Santino Hassell" rel="nofollow noopener">Afterimage</a>, <a href="http://jgenao.wordpress.com/2013/06/09/afterimage/" rel="nofollow noopener">and blogged about it</a>, but spent most of my post whining about how much of a chickenshit motherfucker I was for not only failing to read the second volume of <i>In the Company of Shadows</i>, but not even reviewing the first one.<br /><br />The results of the poll on that page pretty much vindicated my cowardice.<br /><br />I read <i>Evenfall</i> not long after <i>Special Forces</i>, for one. And winter is a historically bad time in Chateau Joolz, and I was all cried-out—and I'd really appreciate it if you guys could just not give me any shit about the blubbering and the wailing, thanks.<br /><br />So, uh—that's why.<br /><br />Mostly.<br /><br />The other reason I never went on to read the next book? I'm writing about assassins too, and somehow they started looking and acting and talking and even <i>fucking</i> like Hsin Liu Vega.<br /><br />All of them.<br /><br />So. Yeah.<br /><br />Then, two weeks ago, someone asked me in an <i>Evenfall</i> thread what my opinion on the book was, and why hadn't I et cetera, and—also—what the hell was wrong with me, anyway?<br /><br /><i>Nothing</i> is wrong with me, okay—look, just—<i>whatever</i>, leave me alone, okay, I'll take care of it, <i>my gosh.</i><br /><br />So here's me taking care of it.<br /><br /><br />***<br /><br /><br />Halfway through reading it I stopped to write Santino Hassell an email. It was a love letter disguised as fan mail.<br /><br />This email was defined by <b>two (2) costly errors in judgement:</b><br /><br />1. <i>My email was too long</i>. I wrote about all the things stewing in my fervid little brain, which had been awakened by his and Ais's writez.<br /><br />and<br /><br />2. <i>My email was a love letter disguised as fan mail</i>.<br /><br />I had tried to corral <i>all the epic feelz</i> the book had set loose, as if that were even possible with a book of this size. Never mind the stupidity of trying to make sense out of any of it when I hadn't even finished it. I was too excited.<br /><br />Mr. Hassell forgave me for that.<br /><br />He forgave me for my second mistake too, cuz he is a cool dude, and was kind enough to never speak of either my knicker-moistening passion or my Caribbean indiscretion, ever again. He even declined to call the cops when I broke the terms of the restraining order and said hi to him at Dunkin Donuts that one time.<br /><br />Buuuuut anyway. <i>Evenfall.</i><br /><br />I learned my lesson. No crazy, all-inclusive review. At over 1,100 words, this still turned out to be the longest review I've ever written—but it's incomplete. No matter how long I make it, my review will <i>always</i> be incomplete, and so I won't even try.<br /><br />These, then, are some of my impressions.<br /><br /><br />***<br /><br /><br /><b>It's long.</b> Half a million words is a lot of words. Some of them don't need to be there. Sometimes the prose is pedantic, or repetitive. Most of the time it's neither of those things.<br /><br /><b>It's fascinating.</b> The world this story unfolds in is layered, rich, and intensely compelling. The premise is solid, and so is the setting. As an example of speculative fiction, it delivers.<br /><br /><b>It's hot as fuck.</b> I touched myself in my Special Place many, many times—I mean... yyyes—<i>obviously</i> I do that all the time anyway—I just meant: <i>while reading this</i>. There were many scenes that were so sensuously drawn I sprang a semi-chub. One of them—the scene featuring a dark room, the pretense of sleep, and stolen underwear? I re-read it so many times in the past six months that I could up the book's goodreads metadata read-count to 16 and not even feel like I was lying.<br /><br /><b>It has Hsin Liu Vega in it.</b> ...no, I didn't say anything else. That's all. Hsin. Hsin Liu Vega. In it.<br /><br /><b>It needs a vicious editor.</b> I'm pretty sure I'm not just being a jealous twat at how productive Ais and Santino are—<i>pretty</i> sure—when I say an old-timey, chain-smoking, liquid-lunch-having Noo Yawk editor would do wonders for this book. I mean, <i>every author</i> needs an editor. Especially the ones who write 3-million-word <i>Epics of Awesomely Epic Awesomeness™</i> entirely on their own over the course of seven years, <i>the fancy bastards</i>.<br /><br /><b>It's got great action.</b> SPOILER, SPOILER, another SPOILER, and holy fuck did you see the SPOILER. (Because a shit-ton of stuff goes down, spectacularly, and with an incredibly-high body-count, this seemed an obvious place to cut things out of my review, to get the word-count down.)<br /><br /><b>It features fun secondary characters.</b> With one notable exception, all the second-tier players are wildly entertaining and memorable. Some are so successful I'm told they go on to carry parts of the tale in subsequent volumes—which tells you how well-crafted they were from the beginning. The exception is Vivienne, who remained disappointingly one-dimensional and cartoonish while still being more or less a <i>heinous bitch.</i> I hope her motivations and decisions are a little less inscrutable and <i>a lot</i> less universally appalling in the next book.<br /><br /><b>Mexico.</b> Sweet, sweet Mexico. By the time this part of the tale arrived I was a wreck of angst and bitterness and anxiety. "Wait until Mexico!" my book buddies advised. "It's all worth it once they get to Mexico."<br /><br />And it was.<br /><br />Because for all the darkness in a dystopian novel like this one—with all the hate and despair and soul-crushing tragedy woven into it; with all the characters and all their victories, and their defeats; with all the death, and all the destruction—all the cold-blooded denial of basic humanity; with <i>all of that</i>, in all those memorable scenes—<i>this is still a romance</i>.<br /><br />And a very good one.<br /><br />Because there's one scene that lives in my memory, still, all these months later. The one scene my mind returns to more often than any other.<br /><br />Even more often than the bit with the underwear.<br /><br />It's the scene on that ancient bus to Mexico, with the sun sinking into the desert, when two lonely, fucked-up young men bump sweaty arms in the heat of a dying day, and for a moment their defenses are down, and the connection they spend so much energy denying is allowed to remain.<br /><br />On that long, somber ride toward the disaster waiting for them on the other side of the horizon, they share a secret between them, these two, surrounded by unknowing strangers with hopes and fears of their own.<br /><br />They share a secret, and—for a little while—they are allowed to keep it.<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>UPDATED 31 MARCH, 2014:<br /><br /><i>this series has been revised and re-released beginning with this volume, evenfall. it is now available for download at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.inthecompanyofshadows.com">http://www.inthecompanyofshadows.com</a></i></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14677060861916073567" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada"><img alt="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583582487p2/12788865.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/770422113?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada">Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Rosalinda *KRASNORADA* by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/7526630-shelley">Shelley</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer770422113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6362624240873932982"><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387310313i/7574436._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>E</b>xhausting<br/><b>V</b>enerable<br/><b>E</b>legant<br/><b>N</b>ecessary. Yeah, you need to read and experience this book.<br/><b>F</b>renetic<br/><b>A</b>MAZING!<br/><b>L</b>ong. <br/><b>L</b>oco!!! This book was completely CRAZY! Or at least, it drove me crazy…<br/><br/>So I finished! I can’t believe it. It took me forever but I finally did it and now I don’t even know how to start this review. Short and nice is always better, right? Ok, let me warn you first. If you haven’t read this book you are NOT allowed to open any spoilers. AT ALL. I’ll find out and will do bad things to you so </span>
  <span id="freeText6362624240873932982" style="display:none"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387310313i/7574436._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>E</b>xhausting<br><b>V</b>enerable<br><b>E</b>legant<br><b>N</b>ecessary. Yeah, you need to read and experience this book.<br><b>F</b>renetic<br><b>A</b>MAZING!<br><b>L</b>ong. <br><b>L</b>oco!!! This book was completely CRAZY! Or at least, it drove me crazy…<br><br>So I finished! I can’t believe it. It took me forever but I finally did it and now I don’t even know how to start this review. Short and nice is always better, right? Ok, let me warn you first. If you haven’t read this book you are NOT allowed to open any spoilers. AT ALL. I’ll find out and will do bad things to you so behave!<br><br>I am going to assume you know what the book is about because I will talk more about my emotions than about the blurb per se. Boyd and Hsin are the main characters in this story and they are forced to work together for the Agency. I don’t know about yourselves but I do love haters-to-lovers stories and this one was by far the absolute BEST. <br><br>Because the book is that long that you really feel how they dislike each other at the beginning and you experience the change in them (I’m having goosebumps now remembering certain parts).<br>I don’t (*didn’t*) read Dystopian so If you have doubts about this one for that reason, please read the book. I promise it was like reading contemp, I promise.<br>While the story is interesting I would say the characters are why this book is so special. I think I had never “seen” characters so perfectly built. <br><br>Boyd is the man of my life. I swear! He’s this little shy kid who doesn’t have friends or a social life. He had a hard life and something happened to him that marked him years ago.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386022610i/7276016.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hsin was not my favourite but I must admit he was a great character. He’s the BEST in his job but he loses it very easily so he needs a partner like Boyd to put him in place? Not sure about that but the thing is they connect and they’re perfect for each other.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386268032i/7326032.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then there are some secondary characters that were awesome and a great addition to the story, specially Ryan. I really hope I’ll get more Ryan in the next book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[With Kassian if possible hehe <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And then there are thoughts in my head that are making me think that Lo Mas Funny and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ someone whose name starts with an E and ends with an O are the same person. Because I know you are still alive, guapo!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>***PLEASE DO NOT OPEN THIS SPOILER*** If you do, this will ruin the book for you </b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>Of course I would never ever ruin a book for anyone. I am going to talk about what I didn’t like and I don’t want people thinking the book is not worth it because it is.<br><br>I am ONLY rating the story, not taking the editing into account but OMG this book needs editing. Anyway, since this is a free read I think I should not complain about this but still. Those 1427 pages were not necessary, there were parts that didn’t add anything to the story.<br><br>Jessica. I can’t remember hating someone as much as I hated her. My poor Boyd!!! And shut up about Thierry!!! He hadn’t even kissed Hsin at that point and he did it because of his job!<br><br>BUT, I read an interview to one of the authors and he said something that makes sense. When you “realize” you like the other team is not like you say “I love the other team so I am not checking out women anymore” so I must admit that Jessica part was necessary. But I still hate her. QUE TE DEN POR CULO, ZORRA!<br><br>And the Spanish parts were very well written, I only saw something incorrect but that’s because I was being a bitch looking for the mistake hehe.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And it's free, AMIG@S!!! Although you can donate some pennies to the authors. Seriously, I cannot read 1427 pages for free!<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.aisylum.com/sonnyais/story.html#bk1">http://www.aisylum.com/sonnyais/story...</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385918151i/7258736.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>P.S. Thanks Shelley for introducing me to this series. Also, thanks for telling me about Pinterest so I could picture the characters ;)<br></i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_405805633" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/405805633" />
    <a title="Kat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4878104-kat"><img alt="Kat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515345527p2/4878104.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/405805633?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat" href="/user/show/4878104-kat">Kat</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kat by: </span>
      how about everyone in The Administration Zone group?
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=war-and-military">war-and-military</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=freefic">freefic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=whine-like-its-1999">whine-like-its-1999</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=a-tsunami-of-angst">a-tsunami-of-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=the-ust-is-strong-in-this-one">the-ust-is-strong-in-this-one</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=waferthin-plot">waferthin-plot</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer405805633" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16609556515464130921">ETA 2018: adjusted my 2.5 star rating to 1 star.<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statement-on-sh'>http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statem...</a><br/><br/>Before jotting down my thoughts, I’d like to post a picture that pretty much captures my current state of mind.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389875i/751242.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was either going to address all my issues in painstaking detail (and this would become an essay) or summarize. I opted for the latter. So after careful consideration of several factors (for example: the tireless effort that obviously went into this 1400-something pages book, the mellowing effect th</span>
  <span id="freeText16609556515464130921" style="display:none">ETA 2018: adjusted my 2.5 star rating to 1 star.<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statement-on-sh">http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statem...</a><br><br>Before jotting down my thoughts, I’d like to post a picture that pretty much captures my current state of mind.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389875i/751242.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was either going to address all my issues in painstaking detail (and this would become an essay) or summarize. I opted for the latter. So after careful consideration of several factors (for example: the tireless effort that obviously went into this 1400-something pages book, the mellowing effect that its m/m-ness and freeness have on me, this thriving, happily fangasming Goodreads community that followed my progress and supported -- and threatened -- me every step of the long, long way) I came to the conclusion that <i>Evenfall</i> deserves 2.5 stars after all.<br><br>Despite...<br>• It being a good 600 pages too long<br>• The extremely limited vocabulary (thousands of references to how everyone’s "irritated", has honey-colored or green eyes, lifts eyebrows etc., that I always think should be less obvious to me, considering that English isn't my native language), the stilted, static writing style (he had to admit that, he couldn’t help thinking that (x1000)).<br>• The continuous, repetitive internal dialog and analysis (see point 1).<br>• The major plot-holes and artificial plot-devices and stupid shizzle, that didn't make sense. Even after I tried to adjust my expectations and view this as uncomplicated pulp instead, it still managed to drive me bug-fuck.<br>• The simplistic, pointless missions that didn't make sense in so many ways (see point 4) and were wrapped up so conveniently.<br>• The lack of character development and interesting dynamics between the two MC's (surprising because of point 1 and 3).<br>• The one-dimensional, mostly "irritated" side characters.<br>• This bizarrely unbelievable clusterfuck of an organization called 'The Agency' (point 4 and 5).<br>• Having to necessarily perfect my skimming skills.<br>• And last but not least, getting behind on my freaking Reading Challenge.:p<br><br>What I did like:<br>• The delicious hype surrounding this series.<br>• The Emo cover kicks ass.<br>• Mexico AKA the sex. It seemed like the writing momentarily picked up during the sex scenes. Or maybe I was just too excited to finally come across something else than bitch-mom's from hell, lethal wounds that heal miraculously and without consequences because it's <i>Da Sin</i>, dude...Boyd's whining... Anyway, I thought the sex scenes were okay and for a change there were no 1..2..3 fingers involved, thank you jesus! Maybe this is just a sign that I'm now an advanced m/m reader, but man, am I getting fed up with fingers aimlessly attempting to loosen up a muscle that just needs a good...well, let's not start talking dirty. So I told my buddy read partner in crime, Day-thief, delightedly that I had finally found something that I did really enjoy about <i>Evenfall</i>. She then brought up <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/670745296" rel="nofollow noopener">a few points</a> that were reason enough for me to reread the sex scenes (hehe! &gt;:-)). And I still liked them, but have to admit that, as is the case with the entire book, they could've been turned into something more, more intense, more brilliant.<br>• The pictures of Hsin and Boyd Lenore showed me. To which I'd like to add a coincidental Tumblr find:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389875i/751243._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the end it turns out that I'm one of those people who stay in a relationship just because the sex is good. So I'll be reading on. Just not right away...<br><br>And finally, it's so comforting to buddy read a hyped book and end up feeling pretty much the same. Thank you Day-thief.&lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="16609556515464130921" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</a><br/><br/>Ok, hand over the medal. I finished. <br/><br/>Look, I’m usually ALL about the instant-gratification. Give me 100’ish pages with a HEA and I’ll give you a smile. So, obvi</span>
  <span id="freeText16774953374845522110" style="display:none"><br><b>ETA: This is a review for the original version of Evenfall. <br><br>The new Directors Cut versions are edited and have some additional content. <br>Evenfall DC pt 1: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20926065-evenfall-vol-1-director-s-cut">https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2...</a><br>Evenfall DC pt 2 (to be released): <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20926136-evenfall-vol-2-director-s-cut">https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2...</a><br><br>Strongly suggest you read these newer versions instead...</b><br><br>**********<br><br><br><a href="http://s1354.beta.photobucket.com/user/syleegurl13/media/ICoS/97e92588-9e38-448f-ba76-dd7c316623bc_zpsc8a24451.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401969i/780775.jpg" alt=" photo 97e92588-9e38-448f-ba76-dd7c316623bc_zpsc8a24451.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ok, hand over the medal. I finished. <br><br>Look, I’m usually ALL about the instant-gratification. Give me 100’ish pages with a HEA and I’ll give you a smile. So, obvi, I was NOT looking forward to devoting myself to 1500 pages of dystopian angst. But, begrudgingly, I began. AND THANK GOD I DID...<br><br>At times it felt torturous, at times it felt painful, at times it felt comedic, at times it felt blissful, at times it felt frustrating, at times it felt like it would never end…at times I wished it would never end…<br><br>Ultimately, it all came down to the strength of the characters. And though I became so connected to Hsin &amp; Boyd that I had a myriad of emotional &amp; physical reactions to their journey…it wasn’t just them. It was ALL of them… strong, interesting, haunting, sympathetic, annoying, aggravating, tender, attractive, fierce characters. And that’s what drives this book…that’s what makes you want to push through 1500 pages…to find out what happens to them…<br><br><u>After Book 1:</u><br><br>Boyd = Brat<br>Hsin = Hperfect<br>Ryan = the pocket version of my dream man<br>Kassian = I’d do you in a heartbeat.<br>Viv = Looked up frigid bitch in the dictionary. It read “see Vivienne Beaulieu”<br>Thierry &amp; Jessica = rage<br><br>Yes, the book dragged at parts, and indeed, it is WAY too long, but still, totally worth the blurry-eyed, sleep-deprived, over-caffeinated 5 days it took me to finish. <br><br>Note to authors (Sonny &amp; Ais): the story is SO MUCH BETTER in the scenes where Sin &amp; Boyd are together…just sayin’. Oh, and I’ve now entrusted you with my heart…please don’t destroy it. </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429479256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10769826860376439877"><br/><br/><b>Caution:</b>This book contains feelings! Fierce, sexy assassins, m/m hot man action, torture and attempted rape. Also...This book is long. So long that it probably would have been quicker for me to skip the length of the Great wall of China than it has taken me to finish this. <br/>I could have read a dozen books in the time I have invested in this book, and it's only book1! <br/>So do I regret any of it? <br/><br/>Oh hell NO! <br/><br/>It grabbed me from the start and at no point did I want to let go. A real two handed handed h</span>
  <span id="freeText10769826860376439877" style="display:none"><br><br><b>Caution:</b>This book contains feelings! Fierce, sexy assassins, m/m hot man action, torture and attempted rape. Also...This book is long. So long that it probably would have been quicker for me to skip the length of the Great wall of China than it has taken me to finish this. <br>I could have read a dozen books in the time I have invested in this book, and it's only book1! <br>So do I regret any of it? <br><br>Oh hell NO! <br><br>It grabbed me from the start and at no point did I want to let go. A real two handed handed hold on tight, white knuckle ride. I was so impressed, like seriously ..just WOW! <br>When it kicks off, oh Jesus...does it ever. It's not just the OH.MY.GOD's. <br>It's all kinds of emotions, fear, anger, loathing, wanting, needing, and sheer desperation that had me squirming and hair pulling. Intense!<br><br>The story is full on, engaging, intriguing, exciting and just plain fabulous. <br>Filled with a paranoid post apocalyptic society of warring government and terrorist factions all set out to destroy each other. It's about twenty years after World War III, and the great nations have just about been wiped out by bombing the crap out of each other. Cities like London, France and New York are pretty much nothing but radioactive wastelands. <br>It creates an intriguing and absorbing atmosphere that really adds to the sense of other worldliness surrounding the characters and plot. Superb!<br><br>Let me introduce you to the MC's Boyd and Sin/Hsin. Meet Boyd... <br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/sexy%20man%20moments/images-3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393578i/757762.jpg" alt="images-3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A young androgonous looking man who has nothing and nobody to live for after an excruciating loss and traumatic experience; he'd given up his desire to to live years ago and with it all sense of hope and a belief in any kind of future. <br>He is emotionless, numb, without a care for life or death and has just become...well...nothing really, until he is ordered by his bitch of a mother to apply for the position of partner to the monster assassin Hsin Vega. A job with zero chance of survival.<br><br>Meet Sin...sexy sexy sexy sexy sexy! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393578i/757763._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 480364_484869751558604_1915298108_n_zps561e97bc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>picture edited 21/06/2013</i><br><br>Holy hell he is just so sexy, did I say sexy already? I am so freaking in love with him! <br>He is tall, broad shouldered, piercing green exotic eyes, fierce and a seriously deadly kick ass heartless (it seems) assassin, with a talent for killing a man dead in 0.03 seconds - while he's tied down!<br> <br>I read a scene where he single handedly murders 40 men in such a graceful almost dance-like display of sheer power and strength...I was spellbound and so turned on! <br>Everybody fears Sin and he is treated like an animal by the agency and it's employees, worse than a dog. He is 28 years old and Boyd is the first person he has ever had a real conversation with. <br><br>Both Boyd and Sin are pawns in a new kind of war. Their fate is held in the barbed and poisonous hands of the agencies leader Marshal Conners, a man who could quite easily put Saddam Hussain and Hitler to shame,a and second in command, Boyd's mother – the bitch whore!<br><br><b>“While yet we live, scarce one short hour perhaps,<br>Between us two let there be peace, both joining,<br>As joined in injuries, and enmity<br>Against a foe by doom express assigned us,<br>That cruel serpent.” <br>― John Milton, Paradise Lost</b><br><br>There is some fantastic character development in this story. Totally unique and original revealings all the way through. Heartbreaking, intense, vivid, orgasmic and just a bloody good book! <br><br>I read every word, and yes it was a struggle at times because Boyd has the need to over analyse <i>everything.</i> <br>His inner monologue drove me crackers but also gave me the answers and understanding needed to understand his, at times rather immature and selfish motives. <br>He is a great guy, who has has been through so much and I really liked him, a lot! But sheesh ...can he gab away in his head! A few times, I was like...alright alright already! Get the hell on with it, you've got your hands down his pants for gawd sake! Just DO something with it! Stop thinking dammit!<br><br>There are a few writing issues and a couple of glaringly obvious inconsistencies and the Spanish dialog lost me for a while. I mean what the hell was up with that? English please or tell me what the hell was just said please. In hind sight I don't think I missed anything vital- but still annoying.<br><br>So will I read the next book? Oh Yes! Most certainly, I just hope Boyd chills out with the inner thought processes.<br><b>3.5 - 4 Stars!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10769826860376439877" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1413475620" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16732124019605529838">I know many are removing their ratings and reviews of all the books they have read, written by Santino Hassell, in light of his despicable behavior. I have deleted my ratings from all Santino books I have read, because I too am shocked and appalled!!! I won't do it with the ICOS series though. I am gonna be honest here and say, that this series is one of the best I have ever read, and I am sure Ais played a big part in my enjoyment. As far as I know, Ais had nothing to do with all that has happe</span>
  <span id="freeText16732124019605529838" style="display:none">I know many are removing their ratings and reviews of all the books they have read, written by Santino Hassell, in light of his despicable behavior. I have deleted my ratings from all Santino books I have read, because I too am shocked and appalled!!! I won't do it with the ICOS series though. I am gonna be honest here and say, that this series is one of the best I have ever read, and I am sure Ais played a big part in my enjoyment. As far as I know, Ais had nothing to do with all that has happend. Until I hear otherwise, my ratings and reviews for this series, will stay up. I am sorry for those who might not agree with me on this. I would also like to say that I am so sorry for all of you who have been hurt....my heart goes out to all of you ;) xoxo<br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/Mind_Blown_zpszswbwean.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467267806ra/19571532.gif" alt=" photo Mind_Blown_zpszswbwean.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Wow....I have no idea how to explain what this book is all about and since there are so many wonderfull reviews out here already, I won't.<br><br>I will say that this book blew my mind. It took me on a freaking rollercoaster ride of emotions. I loved the two MC's, yet hated them at the same time..lol. I can't tell you which one of them I liked best, because it kept changing.... Let's just say that both Boyd and Sin were awesome !!<br><br>This book is very very long. My dear friends, told me to read the long version instead of the directors cut, because I wouldn't want to miss anything....and they were right !! It was long, but there wasn't a moment that I was bored. I ate it all up...all 1400 + pages ;)<br><br>I laughed, I cried, I cursed (a lot) and I swooned. These boys were epic and very very sexy :D<br><br>I do have to note that eventhough this wasn't a buddy read, I wouldn't have survived wihout the support of my dutch girls...lol. Thank you Susan and Elsbeth for being on stand by !! :D<br>I'm gonna need you guys again for book 2 !!!<br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/2452796tkury9pmjq_zpsgk7ou1ve.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467267806ra/19571533.gif" alt=" photo 2452796tkury9pmjq_zpsgk7ou1ve.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ofcourse I'm gonna jump into book 2 right away, because after all these pages I feel like I already know them so well. I can't wait to read what happens next, though a little birdie told me that book 2 was the most angsty.....<br><br>5 stars for this awesome book with it's awesome characters !!<br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/17503230_zpsghwanu2f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467267806ra/19571534.gif" alt=" photo 17503230_zpsghwanu2f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_505346556" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/505346556" />
    <a title="Steph" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4215697-steph"><img alt="Steph" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346102450p2/4215697.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/505346556?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steph" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steph" href="/user/show/4215697-steph">Steph</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=provided-by-author">provided-by-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=kindle-read">kindle-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=favorites-2015-and-before">favorites-2015-and-before</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer505346556" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11711560696149808216"> I was a little afraid to start reading this book if I'm completely honest. At 1427 pages, it is the longest book I have ever read, by a mile. That alone is pretty daunting. LOL<br/> I had heard some pretty great things about this series, but nothing could've prepared me for just how much I loved it.<br/><br/> <b>Evenfall took over my whole life, for six wonderful days.</b> My poor hubby got ignored, my house was a complete damn mess, food wasn't really that important anymore, or sleep. Who needs it, really? My house</span>
  <span id="freeText11711560696149808216" style="display:none"> I was a little afraid to start reading this book if I'm completely honest. At 1427 pages, it is the longest book I have ever read, by a mile. That alone is pretty daunting. LOL<br /> I had heard some pretty great things about this series, but nothing could've prepared me for just how much I loved it.<br /><br /> <b>Evenfall took over my whole life, for six wonderful days.</b> My poor hubby got ignored, my house was a complete damn mess, food wasn't really that important anymore, or sleep. Who needs it, really? My house could've been falling down around me and I wouldn't even have cared. LOL<br /><br /> I am struggling to know what to say. I want everyone to know that this book is absolutely incredible, but I don't know if anything I say will do it justice.<br /> This is one good way to show how much I liked it... I made 99 highlights on my Kindle, and that was edited, a lot! I wanted to highlight something on every single page. Also, I hit a new record of progress updates too. There were so many amazing things that happened, so many twists and turns.<br /> I loved every single word, every single page. <br /><br /> Okay, moving on to the characters.<br /><br /> I have to start with Hsin/Sin Vega. I'll give you a quick run-down on him, some facts...<br /> Sin was trained to be an assassin, by his father Emilio, when he was just eight years old. He wanted Sin to be just like him but without any of his weaknesses, leading to a very harsh and abusive childhood.<br /> Sin's father died when he was fourteen years old, that's when Sin took over his position at The Agency. He was the perfect assassin, just like Emilio had trained him to be. But it eventually became clear that his past and all the abuse he suffered, could never be forgotten. It's there in his head all the time. When faced with any form of abuse, whether it's against himself or seeing someone else in that position, he takes very drastic action. Leading him into some terrible situations where he kills anyone that comes close to him. <br /> Everyone in the Agency seems to hate him; they judge him based on his past actions because they're too afraid of him and refuse to get to know him now. They Agency call him 'The Monster', and when he does lose control they use the one weakness they know about, claustrophobia, to control him. They lock him away in a box for months at a time and drug him when he becomes distressed. Then they wonder why he comes out swinging? They're the monsters.<br /> <br /> This is where we meet Boyd Beaulieu. He has been put forward by his Agency Official mother, Vivienne, to be Sins new partner. His job is to be Sin's back-up. To stand back and allow Sin to do his job, but to stop him from killing people unnecessarily, to stop him from doing anything that he hasn't been asked to do.<br /><br /> <b>********** Spoilers Ahead, read ahead at your own risk. ************</b><br /><br /> Boyd is a really wonderful character. It's very difficult to remember that he is only nineteen years old. Boyd is just as messed up as his new partner, but for very different reasons. He lived through a very brutal and violent attack by a street gang a few years ago. He was forced to watch a lover be murdered, right before his eyes; he was pinned to the ground while they whispered true horrors in his ears. Leaving him scarred for life. Boyd has been alone and lost for so long, just letting his life pass him by. Not really living at all. <br /><br /> <i>Now onto the best part of the entire book, Sin and Boyd together!</i><br />(There's a ridiculous grin on my face right now. LOL)<br /><br /> I will admit that by like 45%, I was starting to get a little frustrated at the lack of sexy time we were seeing. <i>*wink wink*</i> But the slow development and realistic build up was truly amazing. Seeing them go from completely ignoring each other, to all the little smiles, the laughing, and the beautiful connection that they forge together. They do this by being themselves. Through trust, honesty and dedication to one another. I loved it.<br /> <br /> Sin -<i>"At first... I realised I didn't want you to die. And then... I realised I wanted to protect you. And then I became very possessive of you, or perhaps the idea of you. I'm still not precisely sure what any of that means."</i> <br /><br /> We had to wait a long time, but when Boyd and Sin do finally come together (pun totally intended, LOL), it's out of this world! They are explosive.<br /> <br /> Sin has a really great sense of humour too...<br /><br /> <i>'Boyd's eyebrows lifted. "Are you calling me psychotic?"<br /> Sin smirked. "You might be. Or masochistic."<br /> "Masochistic?" Boyd echoed in a drawl, his lips lifting into a wry smile. "You think so?"<br /> "You must be if you want to screw around with a half deranged assassin," he replied with a raised brow.'</i> <br /> Bwahahahaha! <br /> <br /> But what I think I loved the most about them was how much they both change, together. They relax more, they talk more and they laugh. They flirt and they tease. That was the reason for my permanent smile throughout this book.<br /> I also loved the huge differences between them. How Sin craves a good fight, whereas Boyd will avoid it if at all possible. Anyway, my point is about how they are when together. Boyd loves that Sin is so fast, so strong and so dangerous, but with him? He takes his time; he gets to know Boyd's body and exactly what he likes. He can be slow and gentle and caring. Boyd relishes the fact that no other person in the world gets to see Sin this was. It's amazing.<br /> <br /> Things are far from simple between them, they have to navigate themselves through situations that most people would never even dream of. Sin doesn't know how to be a friend, or a lover. Things that to him are normal, that he thinks will help, are not generally acceptable. He has to learn the difference, which is really hard.<br /><br /> <i>"He was a helpless, emaciated, fucking drug addict. And I ripped him apart because of what he did to you, and you -- you just treat me like I'm a freak, and you sit there in my face and make nice with Thierry and let him take you home and fuck you."</i><br /><br /> While they had their problems, this relationship is just beautiful to watch. <br /> When things go seriously wrong, I was so happy that they both foght for what they wanted, each other. They don't mess around or let the other think things that aren't true...<br /><br /> Sin - <i>"I don't want to go back to the way I fucking was. I don't want to go back to being alone and having to be nothing but a weapon. I don't want to pretend that I don't --" He stopped again and realised with a sense of humiliation that he was about to display the ultimate form of human weakness. <br /> "I can't do it without you," he grit out. "I won't."</i><br /><br /> The cast of secondary characters were brilliant and so well done. There was the perfect amount of back ground detail so we could connect them with the story.<br /> <br /> Vivienne (Boyd's mother) really is a terrible, terrible person. I hate the way she makes Boyd feel so worthless. Like he has nothing to live for and that no one would miss him if he was no longer here. The more we got to know her, the more I hated her.<br /> <br /> Ryan was such a darling. It was so sweet that he had such a crush on Sin, but also that he was Sin's friend, whether Sin knew it or not. He looks out for Sin and now Boyd. He cares about how they are treated and helps them whenever he can. He's a great friend.<br /><br /> I really enjoyed learning all about this world that Sonny and Ais have created, some years in the future after another world war. The stories and the missions are so clever and detailed.<br /><br /> Now, I have to stop there otherwise there will be nothing left for you all to read. <i>Sorry I got carried away, again!</i> LOL<br /> <br /> I honestly don't think I will find another book I love quite as much as this one, in 2013. It was everything I look for in a book, and so, so much more.<br /><br /> <i>*Huge thanks to Em and Giorgia. This book wouldn't have been the same without you both.*</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="11711560696149808216" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/496138990" />
    <a title="Kristalia " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5705623-kristalia"><img alt="Kristalia " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1535637983p2/5705623.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/496138990?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristalia " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristalia " href="/user/show/5705623-kristalia">Kristalia </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer496138990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9480509533000487868"><b>Final rating: 4.5/5 stars</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403642ra/785292.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b> edit: MWAHAHAH UPDATED THE REVIEW WITH PICS FOR SIN AND BOYD ♥</b><br/><br/><b>4.5 stars</b> only because it was <b> freaking long - and officially the longest book i have ever read</b>!!! Other than that, this book is just <b>perfect</b>, and so far, the best <b> mm i have ever read</b>. <br/><br/>The story was very cool, it had action, stealth missions, seductions and whatever else; but the main point was once again-in characters, who were so perfect that i have no words for. Actually - they are one of <b>the most belie</b></span>
  <span id="freeText9480509533000487868" style="display:none"><b>Final rating: 4.5/5 stars</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403642ra/785292.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b> edit: MWAHAHAH UPDATED THE REVIEW WITH PICS FOR SIN AND BOYD ♥</b><br><br><b>4.5 stars</b> only because it was <b> freaking long - and officially the longest book i have ever read</b>!!! Other than that, this book is just <b>perfect</b>, and so far, the best <b> mm i have ever read</b>. <br><br>The story was very cool, it had action, stealth missions, seductions and whatever else; but the main point was once again-in characters, who were so perfect that i have no words for. Actually - they are one of <b>the most believable set of characters ever.</b> Anyway, it was just fantastic.(especially for those who love tortured heroes[both of the MC are]). <br><br>And another thing for 4.5 stars =&gt; <b>sometimes there were to many descriptions of surroundings and such.</b><br><br>Soooooooooo......<b>it's worth of reading,</b> though you have to have patience to read this enormous book and it's way to long chapters. But it was worth every page of it :D<br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>CHARACTERS</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br>There were many of them in the book. And so many worth remembering. Except for Sin and Boyd (our hot male duo) there are also many many more who are important for the story. Most of them i wanted to kill though. Except Ryan - he was way to adorable!!!!<br><br><blockquote> "After all, a life without living was simply a death without dying. What more was there to fear or hate but life, endless life, with no respite?" </blockquote><br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Boyd</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403642i/785293.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the beginning he is represented as quite emotionless blondie,who was chosen to be Sin's partner. And, that practically meant a willing death sentence, since Sin's reputation spoke that his partners didn't live long. Or at all, if he didn't kill them first. But since Boyd didn't have anything left to lose, he accepted the role. After a while we do see that he after all, has feelings and fears but he is afraid of showing them. Since his mother is one of the heads of the agency, everybody underestimated him always, and he was so-so in almost the same situation as Sin. But unlike everyone else, he thought he could get to know Sin from the inside. Which he eventually succeeded. He also had really tortured past, and unlike the standard tortured heroes pasts. His was more complicated and in more ways always had quite psychological consequences. The only thing i hated about him: he is way to observing stuff. To much info for my brain sometimes... <br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Sin</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403642i/785294.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kick ass. Serious, kick-ass-Asian-super-awesome-green-eyed-abso-f*cking-lutely-mothafakaaaaa xDDD.... is also my poor poor baby. <br><br> <br><br>Many people consider him a monster,and in retaliation they treat him as an animal. Sometimes he has bad "episodes" where he gloriously kills dozen people - without weapons sometimes. And all of that because he can't stand someone being abused, but when it comes to him, he will tolerate it until he cracks...and he has strong pain endurance, which makes people (sadists) hurt him even more. These episodes of his also happen every time that Sin can't withstand their torture. They never treated him as a human, even though he is the agency best agent-assassin ever. So, in the end, they abuse him, torture him both mentally and physically, and they use his fear of claustrophobia against him so they can control him. (erm...if he was a monster he wouldn't have fears, right? F*ck logic, huh???)....AAAAAAnd, he would never be considered as a monster if they just gave him a chance, and no one ever did. Except for Boyd. He truly understood Sin, and he has never hurt him. Oh and if Boyd past was unique enough, Sin's even more....oh, and not just past, everything is happening in the present as well, and i wonder how he is still sane after all that has happened to him, or what had been done to him. And yet, he is still loyal to the agency. Poor guy.<br><br>Other than that, when you see through Sin's eyes, you see just how absolutely adorable he is (when he is not in his killing spree mode xD)...<br><br>And every time something happens to him i was swept by the wave of feels.<br><br>♦ Actually <b>
  <i> their relationship </i>
</b> is not love at the first sight, or love by looks. They both take their time to open to each other, and they are both stubborn and in many ways similar, though it takes many of chapters for them to actually admit it. <b>So, there was no insta love, there was only insta-hate at the beginning.</b><br><br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>OVERALL</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br>And, i need to read second book, but there are so many which *puppy eye* me, so it will have to wait for a while.<br><br><b>

</b><br><a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/2013/04/evenfall-in-company-of-shadows-1-by-ais.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380363317i/714576.png" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_2054158911" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2054158911" />
    <a title="Deborah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24383684-deborah"><img alt="Deborah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515068567p2/24383684.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2054158911?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deborah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deborah" href="/user/show/24383684-deborah">Deborah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2054158911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4278057458022649740">Words fail me as to just how unbelievably brilliant this book is.<br/><br/>Having read the Directors Cut back in 2016 I always intended to read the original version. <br/>Firstly I had to actually get my hands on a copy since it’s no longer available (thanks Christelle) once I had my copy I needed time to read and enjoy and decided this would be my Christmas present to myself.<br/>This book is long and I do mean long (1427 pages) that’s a lot of reading especially when you consider that<br/>Evenfall 1 (Director’s Cut) i</span>
  <span id="freeText4278057458022649740" style="display:none">Words fail me as to just how unbelievably brilliant this book is.<br /><br />Having read the Directors Cut back in 2016 I always intended to read the original version. <br />Firstly I had to actually get my hands on a copy since it’s no longer available (thanks Christelle) once I had my copy I needed time to read and enjoy and decided this would be my Christmas present to myself.<br />This book is long and I do mean long (1427 pages) that’s a lot of reading especially when you consider that<br />Evenfall 1 (Director’s Cut) is 334 pages<br />Evenfall 2 (Director’s Cut) is 344 pages<br />That’s a lot of extra pages but I read every word on every page, I never once considered skimming or skipping. I was mesmerised completely and utterly.<br /><br />Nothing I write will come close to describing this book, how it made me feel and the extent to which I totally lost myself in it. The feelings it evoked in me (I think I went through the whole spectrum) it’s frustrating as hell at times and the misunderstandings and lack of communication drove me crazy. <br /><br />It's set in the post-apocalyptic future where the Agency works covertly to protect the current government. Doing anything that it deems necessary using whatever means it has available.<br />Hsin Liu Vega or Sin as he’s known is the Agency's most efficient killer, he's a living legend surrounded my mystery and fear, he's a killing machine they find difficult to control.<br />When we first encounter Sin he's being kept unconscious in a box. Sin is claustrophobic and has spent the last six months in a six feet by five feet metal box. Sin is over six feet tall.<br /><br /><i>Slumping against the sterile floor, the man appeared to be in his twenties and was heavily restrained. He wore only close-fitting black shorts so his body was completely displayed to the heavily armored men that surrounded him. He was sleekly muscular and incredibly well-toned despite his slender build. His light olive-toned skin was marred by horrific-looking scars, gashes, what had obviously been bullet holes, and a tattoo. Hsin Liu Vega, or Sin as he was widely referred to in the Agency, was emaciated and had a wild look about him.</i><br /><br />They also need a partner for him since all his previous partners have ended up dead and this is how we meet Boyd. Boyd is different, for a start he's not from the Agency although his mother is, he's closed off and most of the time it appears he has zero personality and this intrigues Sin.<br /><br />As Boyd and Sin grow close we discover a fun side to Sin and we see how good these two are together. Before Boyd he never had a reason to smile, his life has been one form of hell or another.<br /><br />The world that's been created here is terrifying brilliant, the Agency and the ruthless way it operates is truly chilling but the story is Sin and Boyd, this is what draws the reader in and doesn't let you go. I just couldn't get enough of these two and I agonised and wanted so much more for them than the life they have.<br /><br />Even though I’ve previously read the Director’s Cut a lot of time it felt like I was <br />reading it for the first time. I was excited and almost to the point of biting my nails and I’ve never bitten my nails, even though I knew what happened I was still anxious and I’d forgotten just how long it takes Sin and Boyd to get their act together.<br /><br />My genre is romance all kinds of romance and that's always without exception the priority for me, now don't get me wrong I like my romance wrapped in a good story but here the writing, the descriptions, secondary characters and just Sin and Boyd themselves managed to pull me into this story to the extent where I'd have kept reading regardless. At one point it looked bleak, okay at several points it looked bleak but I realised I was so into this book that even if the relationship fell away I'd still be reading and while you might think this is obvious it's the first time I remember it happening to me. Although I have to say I would not have been a happy bunny.<br /><br />This mission is their most difficult yet and it makes for an agonising read at times, Sin and Boyd find themselves in Mexico set up in a crappy apartment Sin is expected to find a job and socialize with people after he's been isolated and treated like an abomination all his life, surely they must realise how difficult this would be for him but they just don't care. <br />Boyd is sent to evaluate the area and find escape routes, which is dangerous in itself when he's deep in drug territory.<br />Have I mentioned how much I hate the Agency?<br />After the scene at the beginning of the book when we encounter Sin in the box I didn't have a lot of love for the Agency, this got worse the more I read and in this book I positively hate the Agency and Connors in particular although it has to be said I have a long mental list of people I want to die and that again has never happened to me before. The treatment of their own agents is unbelievable and I wanted something dreadful to happen to a lot of them.<br /><br />This book is simply amazing and it’s almost impossible to pick out any best bits but these two made me smile, along with many others I might add.<br /><br /><i>"I figured you'd be dead by now. It's surprising and I'm very rarely surprised." <br /><br />"Oh not at all," and this time the sarcasm was dripping from Boyd's tone. "Why don't I just go out there," he pointed toward the door as if Sin could not understand, "and walk into the wall a few times, maybe crouch in the light more than shadows. You know, lure him out with my ineptitude. I could also have my pants undone for easy access castration. This sounds like a good plan."</i><br /><br />It’s straight into Afterimage for me and I have mixed feelings about this. While it is undeniably brilliant I spent a large chunk of it annoyed and upset with Boyd, let’s hope it’s easier the second time round.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4278057458022649740" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6878524101660075247">I finished this wonderful book (old version) last night at 1 a.m. and I was wondering for a long time haw to rate it... <br/>I was somehow emotional and I just didn't have the strength to write this review.<br/>But now I am ready. SO ...<br/>5 BIG stars because I couldn't go to sleep so many nights until 4.30 a.m. but than woke up at 7 to go to work. <br/>5 stars because I loved SIN!!! And SIN & Boyd together <3<br/>5 stars because it was one of the most terrific stories I've read so far!<br/>This book kept me awake at night</span>
  <span id="freeText6878524101660075247" style="display:none">I finished this wonderful book (old version) last night at 1 a.m. and I was wondering for a long time haw to rate it... <br />I was somehow emotional and I just didn't have the strength to write this review.<br />But now I am ready. SO ...<br />5 BIG stars because I couldn't go to sleep so many nights until 4.30 a.m. but than woke up at 7 to go to work. <br />5 stars because I loved SIN!!! And SIN &amp; Boyd together &lt;3<br />5 stars because it was one of the most terrific stories I've read so far!<br />This book kept me awake at night for so many hours... I just couldn't put it down!!!<br />From the beginning I was so attracted to SIN, but it was more than curiosity... He made me want to discover his story and read more, just to discover more of him and his life, his past, his story.<br />Boyd.. hmm. He made me imagine him as a very cute, but somehow broken man. He made me like him and want to discover his past too. <br />Together they made such a good team and more than that. It was somehow one of the best couples I've read about. The tension was HUGE! <br />It was the biggest/longest book I've read so far, with a lot of action and the scenes were somehow so real. God, I imagined them and everything...<br />So, I can't wait to read more and I just can't let them go!<br />So... 5 emotional stars!<br /></span>
